📝 用户要求将一段关于Windows PowerPC堆栈检查函数的英文技术文档翻译成中文，同时保留英文专有名词。让我仔细分析这段文字： 1. 这是一段技术文档，描述了Windows在PowerPC架构上的堆栈检查函数实现 2. 包含汇编代码注释和技术细节 3. 需要保留专有名词如PowerPC、Windows、TEB等 让我逐段翻译： "We continue our historical survey of Windows stack-checking functions by looking at the PowerPC." 我们继续对Windows堆栈检查函数进行历史回顾，这次来看PowerPC。 "The weird thing here is that on PowerPC, you ask for the negative of the stack frame size. We'll see why soon." 这里奇怪的是，在PowerPC上，你需要请求堆栈帧大小的负数。我们很快就会明白为什么。 "; on entry, r12 is the *negative* of the number of bytes to allocate" ; 进入时，r12是待分配字节数的*负数* "; on exit, stack has been validated (but not adjusted)" ; 退出时，堆栈已验证（但未调整） "chkstk: subi r0, r12, PAGE_SIZE - 1" chkstk: subi r0, r12, PAGE_SIZE - 1 "; expand by another page to make sure we get it all" ; 再扩展一页以确保获取全部 "; get the stack limit for the current stack" ; 获取当前堆栈的堆栈限制 I compare the stack pointer to zero, which helps determine the type of stack being used. By adding the result to the stack pointer, I can calculate a proposed new stack limit. If the result is non-negative, it indicates a user mode stack. The comparison helps distinguish between user and kernel stack environments, which is crucial for proper memory management on the PowerPC architecture. I retrieve the kernel thread state and examine its stack starting point. By subtracting the kernel stack size, I determine the stack's end location. For user mode, I load the stack limit directly from the Thread Environment Block (TEB), which provides critical memory boundary information. I calculate the required stack growth by comparing the current stack pointer against the defined stack limit. This helps prevent stack overflow and ensures sufficient memory is available for the current execution context. I convert the needed stack growth from bytes to pages by right-shifting 12 bits, which effectively divides the memory requirement by 4096. If no additional space is needed, I return immediately. Otherwise, I prepare to loop through and touch memory pages to ensure stack expansion is possible. I incrementally touch pages by loading from decreasing memory addresses, probing the stack's growth potential. Each iteration adjusts the stack limit, systematically verifying memory accessibility. Once the probing is complete, I return from the subroutine, having confirmed stack expansion feasibility. Similar to the MIPS implementation, this code efficiently handles scenarios where stack growth is unnecessary. However, determining stack limits requires analyzing the stack pointer's characteristics, distinguishing between user-mode and kernel-mode stack configurations. The approach leverages PowerPC's unique kernel/user stack segmentation, utilizing thread state information to dynamically manage stack boundaries. 我们继续对Windows堆栈检查函数进行历史回顾，这次来看PowerPC。奇怪的是，在PowerPC上，你需要请求堆栈帧大小的负数。我们很快就会明白为什么。 ; 进入时，r12是待分配字节数的*负数* ; 退出时，堆栈已验证（但未调整） chkstk: subi r0, r12, PAGE_SIZE - 1 ; 再扩展一页以确保获取全部 ; 获取当前堆栈的堆栈限制 cmpwi sp, 0 ; 检查我们使用的是哪种堆栈¹ add r0, r0, sp ; r0 = 提议的新堆栈限制 bge+ usermode ; 非负表示用户模式 mfsprg r11, 1 ; 获取内核线程状态 lwz r11, StackStart(r11) ; 堆栈起始位置 subi r11, r11, KERNEL_STACK_SIZE ; 堆栈结束位置 b havelimit usermode: lwz r11, StackLimit(r13) ; 从TEB获取堆栈限制 havelimit: sub r0, r11, r0 ; r0 = 所需的堆栈增长字节数 srawi. r0, r0, 12 ; r0 = 所需的堆栈增长页数 blelr ; 如果≤0，则无需操作 mtctr r0 ; 准备循环 probe: lwzu r0, -PAGE_SIZE(r11) ; 访问一页并调整r11 bdnz probe ; 持续访问 blr ; 返回 与MIPS版本一样，这段代码在堆栈已经增长到足以容纳分配的情况下会短路处理，但为了进行计算，它必须知道堆栈限制在哪里，而这又意味着要探测堆栈指针来判断它是用户模式堆栈还是内核模式堆栈。这依赖于PowerPC上内核/用户堆栈分割的事实。

📝 首先，用户要求将这段英文翻译成中文，同时保留英文专有名词。专有名词如80386、MIPS、x86-32等应该保留英文。 段落内容是关于栈探测（stack probing）的技术解释，涉及80386和MIPS处理器的差异。 我需要先理解整段意思，然后翻译成流畅的中文。 原文： "Last time, we looked at how the 80386 performed stack probing on entry to a function with a large local frame. Today we’ll look at MIPS, which differs in a few ways. ; on entry, t8 = desired stack allocation chkstk: sw t7, 0(sp) ; preserve register sw t8, 4(sp) ; save allocation size sw t9, 8(sp) ; preserve register li t9, PerProcessorData ; prepare to get thread bounds bgez sp, usermode ; branch if running in user mode subu t8, sp, t8 ; t8 = new stack pointer (in delay slot) lw t9, KernelStackStart b havelimit subu t9, t9, KERNEL_STACK_SIZE ; t9 = end of stack (in delay slot) usermode: lw t9, Teb(t9) ; get pointer to current thread data nop ; stall on memory load lw t9, StackLimit(t9) ; t9 = end of stack nop ; burn the delay slot havelimit: sltu t7, t8, t9 ; need to grow the stack? beq zero, t7, done ; N: then nothing to do li t7, -PAGE_SIZE ; prepare mask (in delay slot) and t8, t8, t7 ; round down to nearest page probe: subu t9, t9, PAGE_SIZE ; move to next page bne t8, t9, probe ; loop until done sw zero, 0(t9) ; touch the memory (in delay slot) done: lw t7, 0(sp) ; restore lw t8, 4(sp) ; restore j ra ; return lw t9, 8(sp) ; restore (in delay slot) The MIPS code is trickier to ready because of the pesky delay slot. Recall that delay slots execute even if the branch is taken.¹ One thing that is different here is that the code short-circuits if the stack has already expanded the necessary amount. 进入时，t8 = 期望的栈分配 chkstk: sw t7, 0(sp) ; 保护寄存器 sw t8, 4(sp) ; 保存分配大小 sw t9, 8(sp) ; 保护寄存器 li t9, PerProcessorData ; 准备获取线程边界 bgez sp, usermode ; 如果在用户模式运行则分支 subu t8, sp, t8 ; t8 = 新的栈指针（在延迟槽中） lw t9, KernelStackStart b havelimit subu t9, t9, KERNEL_STACK_SIZE ; 📝 The user wants me to translate a Dutch text to Chinese, while retaining English proper nouns. Let me analyze the text: "De belastingdienst is van plan om de BTW uit te besteden aan een Amerikaans bedrijf, wat echt waanzinnig is. Op 19 maart is er een commissievergadering in de Tweede Kamer hierover, en ik hoop van harte dat men bij zinnen komt.
